route-policy ALL
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy mark
  if community matches-any sol then
    set local-preference 170
  endif
  if destination in (194.27.222.0/24) then
    set local-preference 170
  endif
  set community ROUTE-KES additive
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy All_Permit
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy Full_Route
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy PERMIT_ANY
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy IKSV_IMPORT
  delete community all
  if destination in (62.244.235.8/32, 84.44.78.192/28) then
    set local-preference 100
    set weight 0
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy IPv6-BGP-LU
  if destination in PFX-ALL-BGP-IPv6-LU-LOOPBACKS then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy YKB_ARCELIK
  if source in (195.87.244.43) and destination in (193.254.228.224) then
    set next-hop 212.156.125.37
  endif
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy netflix-test
  delete community all
  if destination in (45.156.12.0/22, 45.156.12.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any VFNET_ERZURUMFTTHISG or community matches-any VFNET-ATAKOY or community matches-any VFNET-GTEPE or community matches-any VFNET-FATIH or community matches-any VFNET-ESENTEPE_FTTH or community matches-any VFNET-CAMLICA-ISG then
    done

    set community VFNET-ESENTEPE_FTTH additive
    set local-preference 200
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy Hsbc_Bank_BGP_Export
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0) then
    done
  endif
  #Reject-Smaller-Than-/24#
  if destination in (0.0.0.0/0 ge 25) then
    drop
  endif
  #remove_rfc1918#
  if destination in (10.0.0.0/8 ge 32, 172.16.0.0/12 ge 32, 192.168.0.0/16 ge 32) then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term#
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Hsbc_Bank_TT_Prefixes then
    done
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks#
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Bgp-Customers#
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    done
  endif
  if as-path in VATHAS_BGP_Customers then
    done
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  if as-path originates-from '15924'  then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!

end-policy

    set community BGP-Customers additive
    done
  endif

    done
  endif

!
route-policy INT_to_INT_EXPORT_V6
  #REJECT BOGONS_V6
  if destination in BOGONS_V6 then
    drop
  endif
  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ###########################################
  if community matches-any ESY_INT1_Arbor_Ozel_Community then
    drop
  endif
  ################################  EXCEPTIONS_END  ###########################################
  #IPTs ROUTEs
  if community matches-any IPT_COMM then
    done
  endif
  #PNI ROUTEs
  if community matches-any PNI_COMM or community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    done
  endif
  #CUSTOMERs ROUTEs
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif
  #LOCAL 
  if as-path in ASN_LOCAL then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT OTHERS
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy INT_to_INT_IMPORT_V6
  pass
end-policy

route-policy INT_to_vRR_EXPORT_V6
  #REJECT BLACKHOLE

    drop
  endif

  if as-path length ge 50 then
    drop

  ################################ EXCEPTIONS_BEGIN ###########################################
  ################################  EXCEPTIONS_END  ###########################################
  #LOOPBACKs TO RR
  if destination in PFX-ALL-BGP-IPv6-LU-LOOPBACKS then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT OTHERS
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy Route_Injection_Test
  if rib-has-route in Default and community matches-every (15924:10000) then
    apply Routes_to_be_injected
    done
  endif
  if community matches-any (15924:100, 15924:10001) then
    done
  endif
  done
end-policy

route-policy to_grid_tier1_export
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any DO-NOT-ANNOUNCE-TNAP then
    drop
  endif
  #Only Announce TC Peering
  if community matches-any TC-Only then
    done
  endif
  #VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY
  if community matches-any VFNET_BLACKHOLE_COMMUNITY then
    drop
  endif
  #NETFACTOR-ANNOUNCE-REJECT
  if destination in NETFACTOR-ANNOUNCE-REJECT then
    drop
  endif
  #IP SLA ANONS ET
  if destination in (31.145.124.0/24, 31.145.162.0/24) then
    done
  endif
  #IP SLA ANONS KES
  if destination in IPSLA_PREFIXES then
    drop
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Prefixes
  if community matches-any From_VF_to_TNAP then
    done
  endif
  #VF_Mobil_Undesired_announce_reject
  if community matches-any From_VF_to_IR or community matches-any From_VF_to_Local then
    drop
  endif
  #Terramark_Kes
  if community matches-any Terramark then
    drop
  endif
  #Reject-Term
  if community matches-any Dont-Announce-to-Customers then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any International-Pops then
    drop
  endif
  #Network-Statements
  if community matches-any Bgp-Main-Network-Statements then
    done
  endif
  #Datacenter-Networks
  if community matches-any Dc-Blocks then
    done
  endif
  #Announce-Bgp-Customers
  if community matches-any Customers then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #Announce-to-Tnap
  if community matches-any Tnap_out then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_allocations
  if community matches-any allocations then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #blackhole
  if community matches-any blackhole then
    done
  endif
  #yurtici_blackhole
  if community matches-any TTNET-Sadece-yurtici then
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_primary
  if community matches-any announce_from_esentepe_atm then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  #esentepe_atm_backup
  if community matches-any announce_from_esentepe_me or community matches-any announce_from_bostanci then
    delete community all
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

    done
